#======================================================================
# Global Action Labels
#
# This section contains the labels for global action controls (e.g., buttons,
# links, tabs, menu items).
#
#  - They are usually imperative verbs or phrases (though not always).
#
#  - If they are nouns, as is the case for tab controls, it usually means
#    "navigate to" or "show" the functionality described by the noun. 
#
#  - If practical, they should be short to keep buttons small.
#
#  - The labels should be capitalized (if applicable).
#
#  - The labels are listed alphabetically by resource key.
#
